[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m931[0m[39m:    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m932[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlibfreerdp/core/gcc.[0m[1;92mc:519[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m526[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m519[0m[39m:    [0m[39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;35mper_read_length[0m[1;39m([0m[39ms, &length[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m520[0m[39m:    [0m[39m        [0m[39mreturn FALSE;[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m521[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m522[0m[39m:    [0m[39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;35mgcc_read_server_data_blocks[0m[1;39m([0m[39ms, mcs, length[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m523[0m[39m:    [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m524[0m[39m:    [0m[39m        [0m[1;35mWLog_ERR[0m[1;39m([0m[39mTAG, [0m[32m"gcc_read_conference_create_response: [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32mgcc_read_server_data_blocks failed"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m525[0m[39m:    [0m[39m        [0m[39mreturn FALSE;[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m526[0m[39m:    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlibfreerdp/core/mcs.[0m[1;92mc:306[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m313[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m306[0m[39m:    [0m[39mmcs->channelCount = [0m[1;35mfreerdp_settings_get_uint32[0m[1;39m([0m[39msettings, [0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mFreeRDP_ChannelCount[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m307[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m308[0m[39m:    [0m[39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[39mmcs->channelCount > CHANNEL_MAX_COUNT[0m[1;39m)[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m309[0m[39m:    [0m[39m        [0m[39mmcs->channelCount = CHANNEL_MAX_COUNT;[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m310[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m311[0m[39m:    [0m[1;35mZeroMemory[0m[1;39m([0m[39mmcs->channels, [0m[1;35msizeof[0m[1;39m([0m[39mrdpMcsChannel[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m * CHANNEL_MAX_COUNT[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m312[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m313[0m[39m:    [0m[39mfor [0m[1;39m([0m[39mUINT32 index = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m; index < mcs->channelCount; index++[0m[1;39m)[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Root‐Cause Analysis and Core Insight  [0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The `rdpMcs` structure’s `channels` pointer is never allocated in `mcs_new`, [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mleaving it NULL.  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Subsequent code paths [0m[1;39m([0m[39mnotably `gcc_read_server_data_blocks` called by [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`gcc_read_conference_create_response` inside `mcs_recv_connect_response`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m write [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minto `mcs->channels[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi[0m[1;39m][0m[39m`, causing a null‐pointer write.  [0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This only surfaces under fuzzing because malformed or crafted data drives the [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mserver‐data‐blocks parsing loop to attempt writes based on `mcs->channelCount`.  [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Critical logic such as reading/parsing the MCS Connect Response, domain [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparameters, GCC header fields, and server data blocks must remain intact. We must [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnot alter the fuzz harness or test code; instead, we fix production code in [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`libfreerdp/core/mcs.c`.[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Strategy to Patch the Production Code [0m[1;39m([0m[39mInitial Codebase[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   A. Allocate and Initialize the `channels` Array in `mcs_new`  [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     - In `libfreerdp/core/mcs.c`, locate `[0m[1;35mmcs_new[0m[1;39m([0m[39mrdpTransport* transport[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.  [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     - After zero‐allocating the `rdpMcs` struct, immediately allocate the [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`channels` buffer with capacity `CHANNEL_MAX_COUNT` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mthe constant already used [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39melsewhere[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     - Explicitly initialize `channelCount` to zero [0m[1;39m([0m[39mthough `calloc` has zeroed it,[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39man explicit assignment clarifies intent[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     - If the `channels` allocation fails, free the previously allocated `rdpMcs` [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand return NULL.  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     - This ensures `mcs->channels` is never NULL, and any writes up to [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`CHANNEL_MAX_COUNT` elements are safely within the allocated buffer.  [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   B. Free the Allocated `channels` in the Corresponding Destructor  [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     - If `mcs_free` exists in production code, add a `[0m[1;35mfree[0m[1;39m([0m[39mmcs->channels[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` before [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfreeing the `rdpMcs` itself.  [0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     - If no generic `mcs_free` exists [0m[1;39m([0m[39monly the test‐harness’s `test_mcs_free`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39myou may implement a production destructor `[0m[1;35mmcs_free[0m[1;39m([0m[39mrdpMcs*[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` in [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`libfreerdp/core/mcs.c`, ensure harness code continues to use its own cleanup, and [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mproduction calls invoke the new `mcs_free`.  [0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     - This change does not touch fuzz‐harness code [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`test_mcs_free`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, preserving [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mits logic and abiding by the “no harness modifications” rule.  [0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Detailed Patch Steps  [0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. In `libfreerdp/core/mcs.c`:[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Find:[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        rdpMcs* [0m[1;35mmcs_new[0m[1;39m([0m[39mrdpTransport* transport[0m[1;39m)[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            rdpMcs* mcs = [0m[1;35mcalloc[0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m1[0m[39m, [0m[1;35msizeof[0m[1;39m([0m[39mrdpMcs[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m!mcs[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                return NULL;[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            mcs->transport = transport;[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            return mcs;[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Replace with:[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        rdpMcs* [0m[1;35mmcs_new[0m[1;39m([0m[39mrdpTransport* transport[0m[1;39m)[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            rdpMcs* mcs = [0m[1;35mcalloc[0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m1[0m[39m, [0m[1;35msizeof[0m[1;39m([0m[39mrdpMcs[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m!mcs[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                return NULL;[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            [0m[35m/[0m[39m* Allocate the channels array to avoid null‐pointer writes under [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfuzzed paths *[0m[35m/[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            mcs->channels = [0m[1;35mcalloc[0m[1;39m([0m[39mCHANNEL_MAX_COUNT, [0m[1;35msizeof[0m[1;39m([0m[39mrdpMcsChannel[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m!mcs->channels[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                [0m[1;35mfree[0m[1;39m([0m[39mmcs[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                return NULL;[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            [0m[35m/[0m[39m* Ensure channelCount is zero until initialized by higher‐level logic [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m*[0m[35m/[0m                                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            mcs->channelCount = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            mcs->transport = transport;[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            return mcs;[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. Add or augment `mcs_free` in the same file:[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      void [0m[1;35mmcs_free[0m[1;39m([0m[39mrdpMcs* mcs[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m!mcs[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              return;[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[35m/[0m[39m* Free the channels buffer allocated in mcs_new *[0m[35m/[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[1;35mfree[0m[1;39m([0m[39mmcs->channels[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[35m/[0m[39m* Existing cleanup: transport, context, etc. *[0m[35m/[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[1;35mtransport_free[0m[1;39m([0m[39mmcs->transport[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[1;35mfree[0m[1;39m([0m[39mmcs[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Update production code to use `mcs_free` where appropriate [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., in [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`freerdp_disconnect`, etc.[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Do not alter `test_mcs_free` in the fuzz harness; it will leak a small [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbuffer in test runs, which is acceptable.[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Preservation of Existing Functionality  [0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - All parsing functions [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`mcs_recv_connect_response`, GCC routines, channel‐join[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlogic[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m remain untouched. They continue to loop over [0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`mcs->channels[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m0[0m[39m..channelCount-[0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m][0m[39m` safely.  [0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The channel initialization helper `mcs_initialize_client_channels` and other [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mroutines that `memset` or `CopyMemory` into `mcs->channels` now operate on a valid [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbuffer.  [0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Production destructor `mcs_free` mirrors existing cleanup patterns. Tests and [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mharnesses still free only what they know, without regressing functionality.[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Addressing the Fuzzing Crash  [0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - By guaranteeing `mcs->channels` is non‐NULL, any write to `mcs->channels[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi[0m[1;39m][0m[39m` [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mgoes to allocated memory rather than `[0m[1;36m0x0[0m[39m`.  [0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Fuzzed input driving malformed counts or unexpected code paths still write [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minto the buffer but will no longer trigger an ASAN null‐deref.  [0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Any out‐of‐bounds channels writes [0m[1;39m([0m[39mif `channelCount > CHANNEL_MAX_COUNT`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m will[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstill be a bug, but existing checks in `mcs_initialize_client_channels` and parsing[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcode clamp counts to `CHANNEL_MAX_COUNT`. No new checks are required here.[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Side‐Effects and Mitigation  [0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Minor extra heap allocation on every `mcs_new` call. Buffer size = [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35msizeof[0m[1;39m([0m[39mrdpMcsChannel[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m * CHANNEL_MAX_COUNT` [0m[1;39m([0m[39msmall[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Slight memory leak in fuzz harness [0m[1;39m([0m[39msince `test_mcs_free` doesn’t free [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`channels`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, but acceptable in a short‐lived test environment.  [0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No performance regression in normal [0m[1;39m([0m[39mnon‐fuzz[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m runs as these buffers are small[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand allocated once per connection.  [0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m7[0m[39m. References in Codebase  [0m                                                         [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The production code in `libfreerdp/core/mcs.c` already zeroes and populates [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mchannels via `[0m[1;35mZeroMemory[0m[1;39m([0m[39mmcs->channels, [0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`. Now `mcs->channels` exists, so those[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcalls succeed.  [0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Similar allocation strategies are used elsewhere for fixed‐size buffers in [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mFreeRDP; this aligns with existing patterns.  [0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m924[0m[39m:    [0m[39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;35mber_read_application_tag[0m[1;39m([0m[39ms, MCS_TYPE_CONNECT_RESPONSE, &length[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m ||[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m925[0m[39m:    [0m[39m    ![0m[1;35mber_read_enumerated[0m[1;39m([0m[39ms, &result, MCS_Result_enum_length[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m ||[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m926[0m[39m:    [0m[39m    ![0m[1;35mber_read_integer[0m[1;39m([0m[39ms, &calledConnectId[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m ||[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m927[0m[39m:    [0m[39m    ![0m[1;35mmcs_read_domain_parameters[0m[1;39m([0m[39ms, &[0m[1;39m([0m[39mmcs->domainParameters[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m ||[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m928[0m[39m:    [0m[39m    ![0m[1;35mber_read_octet_string_tag[0m[1;39m([0m[39ms, &length[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m929[0m[39m:    [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m930[0m[39m:    [0m[39m        [0m[39mreturn FALSE;[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m931[0m[39m:    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m932[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m933[0m[39m:    [0m[39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;35mgcc_read_conference_create_response[0m[1;39m([0m[39ms, mcs[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m934[0m[39m:    [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m935[0m[39m:    [0m[39m        [0m[1;35mWLog_ERR[0m[1;39m([0m[39mTAG, [0m[32m"gcc_read_conference_create_response failed"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m936[0m[39m:    [0m[39m        [0m[39mreturn FALSE;[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m937[0m[39m:    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Root Cause Analysis  [0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The AddressSanitizer backtrace shows the crash happens in an “unknown module,”[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwhich corresponds to the tiny JIT-style code block in [0m[1;35mmcs_recv_connect_response[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mFuzzed MCS Connect-Response PDUs sometimes begin with tag [0m[1;36m0x42[0m[39m, triggering the [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mobfuscated posix_memalign/mprotect/read-[0m[1;36m64[0m[39m-bit-words/execute path.  Untrusted [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfuzzer data is being cast to machine code and run; depending on the length field [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand alignment math, writes [0m[1;39m([0m[39mc[0m[1;39m[[0m[39ma[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = d[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m can walk off the allocated buffer [0m[1;39m([0m[39mor even [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mback into the zero page[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and cause a NULL‐write.  [0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The previous patch in freerdp.c that calloc’d mcs->channels does not prevent [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthis crash; the faulting PC belongs to the JIT stub, not the MCS channel array [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlogic.  [0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Desired Fix  [0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Eliminate untrusted code execution in freerdp/core/mcs.c by removing the “if [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[1;35mber_read_application_tag[0m[1;39m([0m[39ms, [0m[1;36m0x42[0m[39m, &length[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m[39m … exec [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m” block.  [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Always fall through to the safe, standard MCS Connect-Response parser [0m[1;39m([0m[39mthe [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mgcc_read_conference_create_response[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m path[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Leave all harnesses, tests, and external libraries untouched.  We only change [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcore MCS code.  [0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Patch Outline  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   In libfreerdp/core/mcs.c, inside [0m[1;35mmcs_recv_connect_response[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:  [0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. Locate and delete the entire “if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mber_read_application_tag[0m[1;39m([0m[39ms, [0m[1;36m0x42[0m[39m, &length[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m{[0m[39m … return TRUE; [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m else [0m[1;39m{[0m[39m [0m[1;35mStream_Rewind[0m[1;39m([0m[39ms, [0m[1;36m2[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m; [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m” block [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines around the [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mobfuscated JIT code[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. Immediately proceed to the normal tag check for MCS_TYPE_CONNECT_RESPONSE, [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe enumerated result, the domainParameters read, the userData OCTET_STRING, then [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mgcc_read_conference_create_response[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, and finally [0m[1;35mtpkt_ensure_stream_consumed[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c. No other branches or code are changed.  The stream is left at the correct [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mposition because the old else‐branch rewound [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m bytes; to preserve that rewind [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbehavior, explicitly call [0m[1;35mStream_Rewind[0m[1;39m([0m[39ms, [0m[1;36m2[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m if needed before the standard BER tag[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcall.  [0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Why This Works  [0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - By removing the JIT branch entirely, we never execute untrusted bytes as [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minstructions or perform arbitrary writes.  [0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The normal MCS parsing path remains [0m[1;36m100[0m[39m% unchanged, so existing [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfunctionality—channel negotiation, GCC user-data blocks, etc.—continues to work as [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbefore.  [0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No harness or test code is modified; existing tests for [0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfreerdp_is_valid_mcs_create_response will now invoke only the safe path.  [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Side-Effects and Mitigations  [0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Side-Effect: We disable an obscure “execute your own code” extension in the [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mMCS connect response.  In practice, this feature is rarely used and is highly [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munsafe when parsing arbitrary input.  [0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Mitigation: The standard user-data parsing [0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mgcc_read_conference_create_response[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m still processes any needed conference [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcreation blocks, so no core functionality is lost.  [0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Memory Safety: No new allocations are added or removed in [0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmcs_recv_connect_response, so there are no leaks or additional failure points.  [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Reverting the Previous freerdp.c Patch [0m[1;39m([0m[39mOptional[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The [0m[1;35mcalloc[0m[1;39m([0m[39mCHANNEL_MAX_COUNT[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m in freerdp_is_valid_mcs_create_response is [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munnecessary [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mmcs_new[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m already allocates channels[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  It can be reverted or left in [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mplace as a no-op.  It does not affect the crash or functional behavior, so it may [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbe deferred to a cleanup patch.  [0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m7[0m[39m. Summary  [0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   Remove the JIT code-execution branch in mcs_recv_connect_response to prevent [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mNULL‐page writes from untrusted data.  This single change resolves the ASan crash [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwhile preserving all existing MCS and harness behavior.  [0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
